title: NSScanner + NSCharacterSet の注意
date: 12/17/2010 00:00:00 AM
categories: iOS NSString
layout: post
---

		<div class="section">
			<p>NSScanner と NSCharacterSet の注意点。iOS 4 前と以後では４バイト文字の扱いが異なりスキャンしてくれない。４バイト文字を扱う場合は気をつけて利用すること。</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">
NSString *key = <span class="synConstant">@&#34;?&#34;</span>; <span class="synComment">//? を４バイト文字にする</span>
NSCharacterSet *cSet = [NSCharacterSet characterSetWithCharactersInString:key];
NSScanner *scanner = [NSScanner scannerWithString:[<span class="synConstant">@&#34;絵文字&#34;</span> stringByAppendingString:key]];

[scanner scanUpToCharactersFromSet:set intoString:<span class="synConstant">nil</span>];
<span class="synStatement">if</span>([scanner scanCharactersFromSet:set intoString:<span class="synConstant">nil</span>]){
    NSLog(<span class="synConstant">@&#34;Hit!&#34;</span>);
}
</pre>

			<p>iOS4 より前だとヒットしない。</p>
		</div>

title: Homebrew に移行してみた
date: 12/24/2010 00:00:00 AM
layout: post
---

		<div class="section">
			<p>MacPorts で入れた ruby 1.9.2 で SSL 認証がうまくいかない。</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">
<span class="synPreProc">#!/usr/bin/env ruby</span>
<span class="synComment"># coding:utf-8</span>

<span class="synPreProc">require</span> <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">net/https</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>

uri = <span class="synIdentifier">URI</span>.parse(<span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">https://www.google.com/</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>)

https = <span class="synIdentifier">Net</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">HTTP</span>.new(uri.host, uri.port)
https.use_ssl = <span class="synConstant">true</span>
https.ca_file = <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">./SVRSecureG2.cer</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span> <span class="synComment"># SSL証明書のパスを書く</span>
https.verify_mode = <span class="synIdentifier">OpenSSL</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">SSL</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">VERIFY_PEER</span>
https.verify_depth = <span class="synConstant">5</span>

https.start <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">https</span>|
  request = <span class="synIdentifier">Net</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">HTTP</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">Get</span>.new(uri.request_uri)
  https.request(request) <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">response</span>|
      response.read_body <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">chunk</span>|
	p chunk
      <span class="synStatement">end</span>
  <span class="synStatement">end</span>
<span class="synStatement">end</span>
</pre>

<pre class="syntax-highlight">
<span class="synSpecial">/</span><span class="synConstant">opt</span><span class="synSpecial">/</span>local/lib/ruby1.<span class="synConstant">9</span>/<span class="synConstant">1.9</span>.<span class="synConstant">1</span>/net/http.rb:<span class="synConstant">677</span><span class="synIdentifier">:in</span> <span class="synSpecial">`</span><span class="synConstant">connect': SSL_connect returned=1 errno=0 state=SSLv3 read server certificate B: certificate verify failed (OpenSSL::SSL::SSLError)</span>
<span class="synConstant">	from /opt/local/lib/ruby1.9/1.9.1/net/http.rb:677:in </span><span class="synSpecial">`</span>connect<span class="synSpecial">'</span>
<span class="synConstant">	from /opt/local/lib/ruby1.9/1.9.1/net/http.rb:637:in `do_start</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
	from /opt/local/lib/ruby1.<span class="synConstant">9</span>/<span class="synConstant">1.9</span>.<span class="synConstant">1</span>/net/http.rb:<span class="synConstant">626</span><span class="synIdentifier">:in</span> <span class="synSpecial">`</span><span class="synConstant">start'</span>
<span class="synConstant">	from testHTTPS.rb:14:in </span><span class="synSpecial">`</span>&#60;main&#62;<span class="synSpecial">'</span>

</pre>

			<p>こんな感じのが動かない。</p>
			<p><a href="http://www.ruby-lang.org/" target="_blank">no title</a> からソースをダウンロードしたらうまくいくし、よくわからない。</p>
			<p>MacPorts は好きなんだけど、サイズが大きすぎるなあと思っていたので Homebrew に移行を始めた。</p>
			<p><a href="https://github.com/mxcl/homebrew/wiki/installation" target="_blank">Installation ? mxcl/homebrew Wiki ? GitHub</a></p>
			<p>こっちの ruby 1.9.2 ではうまく動いた。</p>
		</div>

---
title: NSLog にさようなら？
date: 01/19/2011 00:00:00 AM
layout: post
---

		<div class="section">
			<h4>NSLog は便利だけど</h4>
			<p>NSLog デバッグはよく使うのだけど、製品版を出すときに削除するのは面倒。</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">
<span class="synPreProc">#define NSLog</span>
</pre>

			<p>みたいにして一括で停止することもできるけど、しっかりやろうとすると DEBUG フラグを作ったりしてやっぱり面倒。それに、ログとして収集したいこともないこともない。</p>
			<h4> GDB デバッガでできる</h4>
			<p>そこで GDB でやってみよう。</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">
NSLog(<span class="synConstant">@&#34;</span><span class="synSpecial">%d</span><span class="synConstant">  Key:</span><span class="synSpecial">%@</span><span class="synConstant">,Value:</span><span class="synSpecial">%@</span><span class="synConstant">&#34;</span>,count,key,value)
</pre>

			<p>みたいなことがしたいなら、ブレークポイントを設定して次のように設定。</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">
<span class="synStatement">printf</span> <span class="synConstant">&#34;%d Key:&#34;</span>, count
po key
<span class="synStatement">printf</span> <span class="synConstant">&#34;, Value:&#34;</span>
po value
<span class="synStatement">continue</span>
</pre>

			<p>最後の "continue" は入れておかないといちいち処理がストップして煩わしいから。</p>
			<h4> 問題も</h4>
			<p>これで OKey! と思いたいのだけど実機でのデバッグ時に動作が重い。そこが問題にならなければこのやり方でやっていこう。</p>
		</div>

title: 特定のユーザへの Mention を取得する
date: 02/04/2011 00:00:00 AM
categories: Ruby Twitter
layout: post
---

		<div class="section">

<pre class="syntax-highlight">
<span class="synPreProc">#!/usr/bin/env ruby</span>
<span class="synComment"># coding:utf-8</span>

<span class="synPreProc">require</span> <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">net/https</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
<span class="synPreProc">require</span> <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">rubygems</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
<span class="synPreProc">require</span> <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">oauth</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
<span class="synPreProc">require</span> <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">json</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>

<span class="synIdentifier">CONSUMER_KEY</span> = <span class="synSpecial">''</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">CONSUMER_SECRET</span> = <span class="synSpecial">''</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">ACCESS_TOKEN</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;&#34;</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">ACCESS_TOKEN_SECRET</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;&#34;</span>


<span class="synPreProc">module </span><span class="synType">Net</span>
  <span class="synPreProc">class </span><span class="synType">HTTPResponse</span>
    <span class="synPreProc">def </span><span class="synIdentifier">each_line</span>(rs = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;\r\n&#34;</span>)
      stream_check
      <span class="synStatement">while</span> line = <span class="synIdentifier">@socket</span>.readuntil(rs)
        <span class="synStatement">yield</span> line
      <span class="synStatement">end</span>
      <span class="synConstant">self</span>
    <span class="synPreProc">end</span>
  <span class="synPreProc">end</span>
<span class="synPreProc">end</span>

consumer = <span class="synIdentifier">OAuth</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">Consumer</span>.new(
  <span class="synIdentifier">CONSUMER_KEY</span>,
  <span class="synIdentifier">CONSUMER_SECRET</span>,
  <span class="synIdentifier">:site</span> =&#62; <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">http://twitter.com</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
)
access_token = <span class="synIdentifier">OAuth</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">AccessToken</span>.new(
  consumer,
  <span class="synIdentifier">ACCESS_TOKEN</span>,
  <span class="synIdentifier">ACCESS_TOKEN_SECRET</span>
)

uri = <span class="synIdentifier">URI</span>.parse(<span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">http://stream.twitter.com/1/statuses/filter.json</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>)

https = <span class="synIdentifier">Net</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">HTTP</span>.new(uri.host, uri.port)

https.start <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">https</span>|
  request = <span class="synIdentifier">Net</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">HTTP</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">Post</span>.new(uri.request_uri)
request.set_form_data({<span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">track</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>=&#62;<span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">@user1,@user2,@user3</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>})
  request.oauth!(https, consumer, access_token) <span class="synComment"># OAuthで認証</span>
  https.request(request) <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">response</span>|
      response.read_body <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">chunk</span>|

        <span class="synComment"># chunked = falseなら例外を発生</span>
        <span class="synStatement">raise</span> <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">Response is not chunked</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span> <span class="synStatement">unless</span> response.chunked?
        <span class="synComment"># JSONのパースに失敗したらスキップして次へ</span>
        status = <span class="synIdentifier">JSON</span>.parse(chunk) <span class="synStatement">rescue</span> <span class="synStatement">next</span>

        <span class="synComment"># textパラメータを含まないものはスキップして次へ</span>
        <span class="synStatement">next</span> <span class="synStatement">unless</span> status[<span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">text</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>]
        user = status[<span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">user</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>]
        puts <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">@</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span> + user[<span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">screen_name</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>] + <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">: </span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span> + status[<span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">text</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>]
      <span class="synStatement">end</span>
  <span class="synStatement">end</span>
<span class="synStatement">end</span>
</pre>

		</div>

---
title: Mac でファイル監視
date: 04/29/2011 00:00:00 AM
categories: Objective-C Cocoa kqueue
layout: post
---

		<div class="section">
			<p>Mac でディレクトリを監視するには FSEvent を使うと楽らしい。ファイルを監視するには File Notification のサンプルなんかを参照するといいみたいだ。</p>
			<p>今回は kqueue/kevent を使ってやってみる。そのために kqueue をラップした UKKQueue を使う。</p>
			<p>やってみたんだけど、どうも WRITE の監視がうまくできないようだ。ファイルのサイズの変更を監視する EXTEND を監視するといいみたい。</p>
			<p>という訳で以下のようなコードを書いてみたよ。gist 使おうかなあ。</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">

<span class="synPreProc">#import </span><span class="synConstant">&#34;UKKQueue.h&#34;</span>

<span class="synStatement">@implementation</span> HTMLPreviewerAppDelegate

@synthesize window;
<span class="synIdentifier">- </span>(<span class="synType">void</span>)applicationDidFinishLaunching:(NSNotification *)aNotification
{
    UKKQueue *queue = [UKKQueue sharedFileWatcher];
    [queue addPathToQueue:fileName notifyingAbout:UKKQueueNotifyAboutSizeIncrease];
    NSNotificationCenter *center = [[NSWorkspace sharedWorkspace] notificationCenter];
<span class="synComment">//    [center addObserver:self selector:@selector(watch:) name:UKFileWatcherAccessRevocationNotification object:nil];</span>
<span class="synComment">//    [center addObserver:self selector:@selector(watch:) name:UKFileWatcherAttributeChangeNotification object:nil];</span>
<span class="synComment">//    [center addObserver:self selector:@selector(watch:) name:UKFileWatcherDeleteNotification object:nil];</span>
<span class="synComment">//    [center addObserver:self selector:@selector(watch:) name:UKFileWatcherLinkCountChangeNotification object:nil];</span>
<span class="synComment">//    [center addObserver:self selector:@selector(watch:) name:UKFileWatcherRenameNotification object:nil];</span>
    [center addObserver:<span class="synStatement">self</span> selector:<span class="synStatement">@selector</span>(watch:) name:UKFileWatcherSizeIncreaseNotification object:<span class="synConstant">nil</span>];
<span class="synComment">//    [center addObserver:self selector:@selector(watch:) name:UKFileWatcherWriteNotification object:nil];</span>
}
<span class="synIdentifier">- </span>(<span class="synType">void</span>)watch:(NSNotification*)note{
    NSString *path = [note.userInfo objectForKey:<span class="synConstant">@&#34;path&#34;</span>];
    UKKQueue *queue = [UKKQueue sharedFileWatcher];
    [queue addPathToQueue:path notifyingAbout:UKKQueueNotifyAboutSizeIncrease];
}
<span class="synStatement">@end</span>
</pre>

			<h4> 参照</h4>

			<ul>
				<li><a href="http://developer.apple.com/jp/documentation/Darwin/Conceptual/FSEvents_ProgGuide/KernelQueues/chapter_6_section_4.html" target="_blank">ファイルシステムイベント プログラミングガイド: 簡単なコード例</a></li>
				<li><a href="http://zathras.de/sourcecode.htm#UKKQueue" target="_blank">Source Code</a></li>
				<li><a href="http://developer.apple.com/library/mac/#samplecode/FileNotification/Introduction/Intro.html#//apple_ref/doc/uid/DTS10003143-Intro-DontLinkElementID_2" target="_blank">Loading&#133;</a></li>
				<li> <a href="http://developer.apple.com/jp/documentation/Darwin/Conceptual/FSEvents_ProgGuide/UsingtheFSEventsFramework/chapter_4_section_3.html" target="_blank">ファイルシステムイベント プログラミングガイド: イベントストリームの作成</a></li>
			</ul>
		</div>

---
title: メールの受信を監視する
date: 06/10/2011 00:00:00 AM
categories: Ruby EventMachine IMAP
layout: post
---

		<div class="section">
			<p>ruby には Net/IMAP という便利な組み込みクラスがあるのだけど、これは EventMachine や Rev を使った方が良いんじゃない？と思いつつ調べてみると EventMachine で実装された em-imap というのがあったので試してみる。</p>
			<p>Net/IMAP</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">
<span class="synPreProc">#! /usr/bin/env ruby</span>
<span class="synPreProc">require</span> <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">net/imap</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">SERVER</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">imap.server</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">USERNAME</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">username</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">PW</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">password</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>

imap = <span class="synIdentifier">Net</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">IMAP</span>.new <span class="synIdentifier">SERVER</span>, <span class="synIdentifier">:ssl</span> =&#62; <span class="synConstant">true</span>
imap.login <span class="synIdentifier">USERNAME</span>, <span class="synIdentifier">PW</span>
imap.select <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">INBOX</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
imap.idle <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">resp</span>| 
  untag = response.name <span class="synStatement">rescue</span> <span class="synConstant">nil</span>
  <span class="synStatement">if</span> untag == <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">RECENT</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
    puts <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">Mailbox now has new messages</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>
  <span class="synStatement">end</span>
<span class="synStatement">end</span>
</pre>

			<p>EM/IMAP</p>
<pre class="syntax-highlight">
<span class="synPreProc">#! /usr/bin/env ruby</span>
<span class="synPreProc">require</span> <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">em-imap</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>

<span class="synIdentifier">SERVER</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">imap.server</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">USERNAME</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">username</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>
<span class="synIdentifier">PW</span> = <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">password</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>

<span class="synIdentifier">EM</span>::run <span class="synStatement">do</span>
  imap = <span class="synIdentifier">EM</span>::<span class="synIdentifier">IMAP</span>.connect(<span class="synIdentifier">SERVER</span>, <span class="synConstant">993</span>, <span class="synConstant">true</span>)
  imap.login(<span class="synIdentifier">USERNAME</span>,<span class="synIdentifier">PW</span>)
  imap.select(<span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">INBOX</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>)
  imap.idle <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">response</span>|
    untag = response.name <span class="synStatement">rescue</span> <span class="synConstant">nil</span>
    <span class="synStatement">if</span> untag == <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">RECENT</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
      puts <span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span><span class="synConstant">Mailbox now has new messages</span><span class="synSpecial">&#34;</span>
    <span class="synStatement">end</span>
  <span class="synStatement">end</span>.errback <span class="synStatement">do</span> |<span class="synIdentifier">e</span>|
    puts <span class="synSpecial">'</span><span class="synConstant">error</span><span class="synSpecial">'</span>
  <span class="synStatement">end</span>
<span class="synStatement">end</span>
</pre>

			<p>CPU／network の比較しようかな。</p>
		</div>

<PAGE_BREAK>
---
title: r92569
date: 08/08/2011 00:00:00 AM
categories: Test262 WebKit
layout: post
---

		<div class="section">
